
### jsonの形

（api名）　getAllRace
（SQL）　select * from t_hourse_race_list order by year,month,day;

http://localhost:8080/getAllRace

### 結局、テーブルは同じなので、出力も同じになる



t_hourse_race_listから出力

（api名）　getAllRace
（SQL）　select * from t_hourse_race_list order by year,month,day;

（api名）　getRaceByYear
（SQL）　select * from t_hourse_race_list where year='<YEAR>' order by year,month,day;





t_hourse_race_resultから出力

（api名）　getSelectedResult
（SQL）　select * from t_hourse_race_result where year='<YEAR>' and month='<MONTH>' and day='<DAY>' and race_name='<RACE_NAME>' order by result;

（api名）　getResultByHourseName
（SQL）　select * from t_hourse_race_result where hourse_name='<HOURSE_NAME>' order by year,month,day;
